    public static final Block YELLOW_WOOL_REDSTONE_TORCH = registerBlock("yellow_wool_redstone_torch", new RedstoneTorchBlock(BlockBehaviour.Properties.ofFullCopy(Blocks.REDSTONE_TORCH)) );
    public static final Block YELLOW_WOOL_REDSTONE_WALL_TORCH = registerBlock("yellow_wool_redstone_wall_torch", new RedstoneWallTorchBlock(BlockBehaviour.Properties.ofFullCopy(Blocks.REDSTONE_WALL_TORCH).dropsLike(YELLOW_WOOL_REDSTONE_TORCH)) );
    public static final Block YELLOW_WOOL_SOUL_TORCH = registerBlock("yellow_wool_soul_torch", new TorchBlock( ParticleTypes.SOUL_FIRE_FLAME, BlockBehaviour.Properties.ofFullCopy(Blocks.SOUL_TORCH)) );
    public static final Block YELLOW_WOOL_SOUL_WALL_TORCH = registerBlock("yellow_wool_soul_wall_torch", new WallTorchBlock(ParticleTypes.SOUL_FIRE_FLAME, BlockBehaviour.Properties.ofFullCopy(Blocks.SOUL_WALL_TORCH).dropsLike(YELLOW_WOOL_SOUL_TORCH)) );

    public static final Block YELLOW_WOOL_WALL_TORCH = registerBlock("yellow_wool_wall_torch", new WallTorchBlock(ParticleTypes.FLAME, BlockBehaviour.Properties.ofFullCopy(Blocks.WALL_TORCH).dropsLike(YELLOW_WOOL_TORCH)) );
